        var apHost = 'https://account.booking.com';

      var halfOfYearMillis = 180 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
      var isIE10orLess = typeof XDomainRequest === 'function';
      var nonGDPR = true;
      var cookiesDomain = (';domain=.' + hostname);
      if (typeof (window.dataLayer) === 'undefined') {
        window.dataLayer = [];
      }
      window.eventCounter = 0;
      
    function getCookie(b) {
      b += "=";
      var e = document.cookie.split(";"), g, h;
      for (g = 0; g < e.length; g += 1) {
        for (h = e[g]; " " == h.charAt(0);)
            h = h.substring(1, h.length);
        if (0 == h.indexOf(b))
            return h.substring(b.length, h.length)
      }
      return null;
    }
      
    function isDefined(consent) {
        return consent && consent !== "undefined";
    }
      
    function convertObjectToConsentString(obj) {
        return Object
            .keys(obj)
            .map(function (key) {
                return key + "=" + obj[key];
            })
            .join("&");
    }
      
    function getHostname() {
      var url = (window && window.location) ? window.location.href : '';
      var hostname = url.indexOf('/') > -1 ? url.split('/')[2] : url.split('/')[0];
      return (hostname.split(':')[0]).split('?')[0];
    }
      
    function updateConsentCookies(consent, alertBoxClosed) {
        if (isDefined(consent)) {

            var consentDate;
            if (isDefined(alertBoxClosed)) {
                consentDate = new Date(alertBoxClosed);
            } else {
                consentDate = new Date();
            }

            // Actual expiration is handled by OT SDK
            var expirationDateMillis = consentDate.getTime() + oneYearMillis;
            var expirationDateString = new Date(expirationDateMillis).toUTCString();

            document.cookie = "OptanonConsent=" + consent + cookiesDomain + ";path=/;expires=" + expirationDateString + ";samesite=lax;";
            if (alertBoxClosed && alertBoxClosed !== 'undefined') {
                document.cookie = "OptanonAlertBoxClosed=" + alertBoxClosed + cookiesDomain + ";path=/;expires=" + expirationDateString + ";samesite=lax;";
            }
        }
    }
      
    function parseConsentToObject(consent) {
        var result = {};
        if (typeof consent === 'string') {
            var parts = consent.split('&');
            parts.forEach(function (part) {
                var keyAndValue = part.split('=');
                result[keyAndValue[0]] = keyAndValue[1];
            });
        }

        return result;
    }
      
    function saveAndSyncImplicitConsent() {
        var optanonObject = parseConsentToObject(getCookie('OptanonConsent'));
        optanonObject.implicitConsentCountry = nonGDPR ? 'nonGDPR' : 'GDPR';
        optanonObject.implicitConsentDate = new Date().getTime();

        var consentStr = convertObjectToConsentString(optanonObject);
        var expirationDateMillis = new Date().getTime() + oneYearMillis;
        var expirationDateString = new Date(expirationDateMillis).toUTCString();
        document.cookie = "OptanonConsent=" + consentStr + cookiesDomain + ";path=/;expires=" + expirationDateString + ";samesite=lax;";
        propagateConsentToOtCrossDomain(consentStr, getCookie('OptanonAlertBoxClosed'));
    }
      
    function sendImplicitConsentToAP() {
        var httpRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();
        httpRequest.withCredentials = true;
        httpRequest.onload = function () {
            if (httpRequest.status === 200) {
                saveAndSyncImplicitConsent(false);
            }
        };
        httpRequest.open('POST', apHost + '/privacy-consents/implicit', true);
        httpRequest.setRequestHeader('Content-type', 'application/json;charset=UTF-8');
        httpRequest.send(JSON.stringify({client_id: 'vO1Kblk7xX9tUn2cpZLS'}));
    }
      
    function updateImplicitConsentIfNeeded() {
        var optanonObject = parseConsentToObject(getCookie('OptanonConsent'));
        var optanonAlertBoxClosed = getCookie('OptanonAlertBoxClosed');
        if (optanonAlertBoxClosed && new Date() - new Date(optanonAlertBoxClosed) <= halfOfYearMillis) {
            return;
        } else {
            if (
                !optanonObject.implicitConsentDate ||
                new Date() - parseInt(optanonObject.implicitConsentDate) >= halfOfYearMillis
            ) {
                sendImplicitConsentToAP();
            } else if (nonGDPR) {
                if (optanonObject.implicitConsentCountry !== 'nonGDPR') {
                    sendImplicitConsentToAP();
                }
            } else if (optanonObject.implicitConsentCountry !== 'GDPR') {
                sendImplicitConsentToAP();
            }
        }
    }
      
    function propagateConsentToOtCrossDomain(consent, alertBoxClosed) {
        var pass_data = {
            'type': 'onetrust',
            'OptanonConsent': consent
        };
        if (alertBoxClosed !== undefined && alertBoxClosed !== null) {
            pass_data.OptanonAlertBoxClosed = alertBoxClosed;
        }
        ['OTcrossDomain'].forEach(id => {
            var IframeOT = window.document.getElementById(id);
            if (IframeOT && IframeOT.contentWindow) {
                IframeOT.contentWindow.postMessage(pass_data, '*');
            }
        });
    }
      
    function OptanonWrapper() {
        if (Optanon && Optanon.GetDomainData() && Optanon.GetDomainData().ShowAlertNotice) {
            for (var i = window.eventCounter; i < window.dataLayer.length; i++) {
                if (window.dataLayer[i].event === "trackOptanonEvent") {
                    var optanonAction = window.dataLayer[i].optanonAction.toLowerCase().replace(/\s/g, "_");
                    if (optanonAction === 'banner_accept_cookies' || optanonAction === 'preferences_allow_all' || optanonAction === 'banner_reject_all' || optanonAction === 'preferences_save_settings') {
                        var alertBoxClosed = getCookie('OptanonAlertBoxClosed');
                        var consent = getCookie('OptanonConsent');

                        var consentObject = parseConsentToObject(consent);
                        var isAnalytical = consentObject.groups.indexOf(analyticalIsAllowed) > -1 ? 1 : 0;
                        var isMarketing = consentObject.groups.indexOf(marketingIsAllowed) > -1 ? 1 : 0;

                        propagateConsentToOtCrossDomain(consent, alertBoxClosed);

                        if (!isIE10orLess) {
                            sendConsentToAP({
                                analytical: isAnalytical,
                                marketing: isMarketing
                            }, updateConsentBackfilledDate.bind(this, consentObject, alertBoxClosed));
                        }
                    }
                }
                window.eventCounter++;
            }
        }
        if (typeof OptanonWrapperCallback === "function" && OptanonWrapperCallback !== "undefined") {
            OptanonWrapperCallback(arguments);
        }
    }
      
    function sendConsentToAP(consent, successCallback) {
        var httpRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();
        httpRequest.withCredentials = true;
        httpRequest.onload = function () {
            if (httpRequest.status === 200) {
                successCallback();
            }
        };
        httpRequest.open('POST', apHost + '/privacy-consents', true);
        httpRequest.setRequestHeader('Content-type', 'application/json;charset=UTF-8');
        httpRequest.send(JSON.stringify(Object.assign({client_id: 'vO1Kblk7xX9tUn2cpZLS'}, consent)));
    }
      
    function updateConsentBackfilledDate(consentObject, alertBoxClosed) {
        consentObject.backfilled_at = new Date().getTime();
        var consentStr = convertObjectToConsentString(consentObject);
        updateConsentCookies(consentStr, alertBoxClosed);
        propagateConsentToOtCrossDomain(consentStr, alertBoxClosed);
    }
      
    function startBackfillingIfNeeded() {
        var consent = getCookie('OptanonConsent');
        var alertBoxClosed = getCookie('OptanonAlertBoxClosed');
        if (isDefined(consent) && isDefined(alertBoxClosed)) {
            var consentObject = parseConsentToObject(consent);
            var consentedAt = new Date(alertBoxClosed);
            if (consentObject.groups && (consentObject.backfilled_at === undefined || new Date(parseInt(consentObject.backfilled_at)) < consentedAt)) {
                var geolocation;
                if (consentObject.geolocation) {
                    var geolocationParts = consentObject.geolocation.split('%3B');
                    geolocation = {
                        country: geolocationParts[0],
                        country_region: geolocationParts[1]
                    };
                }

                sendConsentToAP(
                    Object.assign({
                        analytical: consentObject.groups.indexOf(analyticalIsAllowed) > -1 ? 1 : 0,
                        marketing: consentObject.groups.indexOf(marketingIsAllowed) > -1 ? 1 : 0,
                        consented_at: consentedAt.toISOString()
                    }, geolocation),
                    updateConsentBackfilledDate.bind(this, consentObject, alertBoxClosed)
                );
            }
        }
    }
      (function(){
        window.addEventListener('message', function(event) {
          if(event && event.data && event.data.name === "OneTrustCookies") {
            updateConsentCookies(event.data.OptanonConsent, event.data.OptanonAlertBoxClosed);
            if (!isIE10orLess) {
              updateImplicitConsentIfNeeded();
              startBackfillingIfNeeded();
            }
            
            if (!nonGDPR) {
              var script = document.createElement('script'); 
              script.type = 'text/javascript'; 
              script.setAttribute('async', 'true');
              script.setAttribute('src', 'https://cdn.cookielaw.org/scripttemplates/otSDKStub.js'); 
              script.setAttribute('charset', 'UTF-8');
              script.setAttribute('data-document-language', 'true');
              script.setAttribute('data-domain-script', domainUUID); 
              document.getElementsByTagName('head').item(0).appendChild(script);
            }
          }
        });
        
        var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
        iframe.src = "https://www.booking.com/cookiebanner.html";
        iframe.id = "OTcrossDomain";
        iframe.frameborder = "0";
        iframe.height = "0";
        iframe.width = "0";
        iframe.style = "position: absolute; overflow: hidden; clip: rect(0 0 0 0); width: 1px; height: 1px; margin: -1px; padding: 0; white-space: nowrap; border: 0; clip-path: inset(100%);";
        iframe.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
        document.body.appendChild(iframe);
      })();
